* Encoding: UTF-8.
*Codes for analysis by SPSS.
* Encoding: UTF-8.
*Explore.
EXAMINE VARIABLES=popul_density urban_percentage schooling SDI gdp HDI HRH 
    allcausemortality HIV_AIDS_a Respirator Enteric_in Neglected_ Other_infe Maternal_a Nutritiona 
    Neoplasms Cardiovasc Chronic_re Digestive_ Neurologic Mental_dis Substance_ Diabetes_a Skin_and_s 
    Musculoske Other_nonc Transport_ Unintentio Selfharm_a Aides__Em Audiologis Dental_Ass Dentistry_ 
    Dentists Dieticians Environmen Medical_As Medical_La Nursing__ Nursing_an Optometris Personal_C 
    Pharmaceut Pharmacist Physical_T physicians__mean Physicians Psychologi Radiograph Traditiona 
  /PLOT BOXPLOT HISTOGRAM NPPLOT 
  /COMPARE GROUPS 
  /PERCENTILES(5,10,25,50,75,90,95) HAVERAGE 
  /STATISTICS DESCRIPTIVES 
  /CINTERVAL 95 
  /MISSING LISTWISE 
  /NOTOTAL.
EXECUTE.

**table 1. 
* Custom Tables.
CTABLES
  /VLABELS VARIABLES=popul_density urban_percentage schooling SDI gdp HDI HRH HRHgroup 
    DISPLAY=LABEL
  /TABLE popul_density [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + urban_percentage [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, 
    PTILE 75] + schooling [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + SDI [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + gdp 
    [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + HDI [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + HRH [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, 
    PTILE 75] BY HRHgroup [C]
  /CATEGORIES VARIABLES=HRHgroup ORDER=A KEY=VALUE EMPTY=INCLUDE TOTAL=YES POSITION=BEFORE
  /CRITERIA CILEVEL=95.
NPAR TESTS
  /K-W=popul_density urban_percentage schooling SDI gdp HDI HRH BY HRHgroup(1 5)
  /MISSING ANALYSIS.
EXECUTE.
* Custom Tables.
CTABLES
  /VLABELS VARIABLES=Aides__Em Audiologis Dental_Ass Dentistry_ Dentists Dieticians Environmen 
    Medical_As Medical_La Nursing__ Nursing_an Optometris Personal_C Pharmaceut Pharmacist Physical_T 
    physicians__mean Physicians Psychologi Radiograph Traditiona HRHgroup 
    DISPLAY=LABEL
  /TABLE Aides__Em [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Audiologis [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Dental_Ass [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Dentistry_ [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Dentists 
    [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Dieticians [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Environmen 
    [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Medical_As [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Medical_La 
    [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Nursing__ [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Nursing_an 
    [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Optometris [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Personal_C 
    [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Pharmaceut [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Pharmacist 
    [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Physical_T [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + physicians__mean 
    [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Physicians [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Psychologi 
    [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Radiograph [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Traditiona 
    [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] BY HRHgroup [C]
  /CATEGORIES VARIABLES=HRHgroup ORDER=A KEY=VALUE EMPTY=INCLUDE TOTAL=YES POSITION=BEFORE
  /CRITERIA CILEVEL=95.
NPAR TESTS
  /K-W=Aides__Em Audiologis Dental_Ass Dentistry_ Dentists Dieticians Environmen 
    Medical_As Medical_La Nursing__ Nursing_an Optometris Personal_C Pharmaceut Pharmacist Physical_T 
    physicians__mean Physicians Psychologi Radiograph Traditiona BY HRHgroup(1 5)
  /MISSING ANALYSIS.
EXECUTE.



**figure 1A and Supplementary Table S5.
*lny to calculate EAPC.
compute HRH_lnp=LN(HRH).
EXECUTE.
*EAPC for total HRHs.
REGRESSION
  /MISSING LISTWISE
  /STATISTICS COEFF OUTS CI(95) R ANOVA
  /CRITERIA=PIN(.05) POUT(.10)
  /NOORIGIN 
  /DEPENDENT 
 HRH_lnp
   /METHOD=ENTER year.
EXECUTE.

*EAPC for total HRHs by country.
SORT CASES  BY location_id_n.
SPLIT FILE LAYERED BY location_id_n.
EXECUTE.
REGRESSION
  /MISSING LISTWISE
  /STATISTICS COEFF OUTS CI(95) R ANOVA
  /CRITERIA=PIN(.05) POUT(.10)
  /NOORIGIN 
  /DEPENDENT 
 HRH_lnp
   /METHOD=ENTER year.
EXECUTE.
SPLIT FILE OFF.
EXECUTE.

*1990.
USE ALL. 
COMPUTE filter_$=(year = 1990). 
VARIABLE LABELS filter_$ 'year = 1990 (FILTER)'. 
VALUE LABELS filter_$ 0 'Not Selected' 1 'Selected'. 
FORMATS filter_$ (f1.0). 
FILTER BY filter_$. 
EXECUTE.
* Custom Tables.
CTABLES
  /VLABELS VARIABLES=location_id_n HRH DISPLAY=LABEL
  /TABLE location_id_n BY HRH [MEDIAN]
  /CATEGORIES VARIABLES=location_id_n ORDER=A KEY=VALUE EMPTY=EXCLUDE
  /CRITERIA CILEVEL=95.
EXECUTE.
USE ALL. 
EXECUTE.

    Maternal_a Nutritiona Neoplasms Cardiovasc Chronic_re Digestive_ Neurologic Mental_dis Substance_ 
    Diabetes_a Skin_and_s Musculoske Other_nonc Transport_ Unintentio Selfharm_a 
    DISPLAY=LABEL
  /TABLE allcausemortality [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + HIV_AIDS_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Respirator [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Enteric_in [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neglected_ 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Other_infe [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Maternal_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Nutritiona [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neoplasms [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Cardiovasc [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Chronic_re [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Digestive_ 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neurologic [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Mental_dis [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Substance_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Diabetes_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Skin_and_s [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Musculoske [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Other_nonc 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Transport_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Unintentio [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Selfharm_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75]
  /CRITERIA CILEVEL=95.
EXECUTE.

* Custom Tables.
CTABLES
  /VLABELS VARIABLES=allcausemortality HIV_AIDS_a Respirator Enteric_in Neglected_ Other_infe 
    Maternal_a Nutritiona Neoplasms Cardiovasc Chronic_re Digestive_ Neurologic Mental_dis Substance_ 
    Diabetes_a Skin_and_s Musculoske Other_nonc Transport_ Unintentio Selfharm_a 
    DISPLAY=LABEL
  /TABLE allcausemortality [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + HIV_AIDS_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Respirator [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Enteric_in [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neglected_ 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Other_infe [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Maternal_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Nutritiona [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neoplasms [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Cardiovasc [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Chronic_re [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Digestive_ 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neurologic [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Mental_dis [MEDIAN, PTILE

  /CRITERIA CILEVEL=95.
EXECUTE.
USE ALL. 
EXECUTE.

*lny to calculate EAPC.
compute allcausemortality_lnp=LN(allcausemortality).
compute HIV_lnp=LN(HIV_AIDS_a).
compute Respirator_lnp=LN(Respirator).
compute Enteric_lnp=LN(Enteric_in).
compute Neglected_lnp=LN(Neglected_).
compute Other_infe_lnp=LN(Other_infe).
compute Maternal_a_lnp=LN(Maternal_a).
compute Nutritiona_lnp=LN(Nutritiona).
compute Neoplasms_lnp=LN(Neoplasms).
compute Cardiovasc_lnp=LN(Cardiovasc).
compute Chronic_re_lnp=LN(Chronic_re).
compute Digestive_lnp=LN(Digestive_).
compute Neurologic_lnp=LN(Neurologic).
compute Mental_dis_lnp=LN(Mental_dis).
compute Substance_lnp=LN(Substance_).
compute Diabetes_a_lnp=LN(Diabetes_a).
compute Skin_lnp=LN(Skin_and_s).
compute Musculoske_lnp=LN(Musculoske).
compute Other_nonc_lnp=LN(Other_nonc).
compute Transport_lnp=LN(Transport_).
compute Unintentio_lnp=LN(Unintentio).
compute Selfharm_lnp=LN(Selfharm_a).
EXECUTE.

*EAPC for all-cause mortality.
REGRESSION
  /MISSING LISTWISE
  /STATISTICS COEFF OUTS CI(95) R ANOVA
  /CRITERIA=PIN(.05) POUT(.10)
  /NOORIGIN 
  /DEPENDENT 
 allcausemortality_lnp
    /METHOD=ENTER year.
EXECUTE.

*EAPC for cause-specific mortality.
REGRESSION
  /MISSING LISTWISE
  /STATISTICS COEFF OUTS CI(95) R ANOVA
  /CRITERIA=PIN(.05) POUT(.10)
  /NOORIGIN 
  /DEPENDENT 
 HIV_lnp
 Respirator_lnp
 Enteric_lnp
 Neglected_lnp
 Other_infe_lnp
 Maternal_a_lnp
 Nutritiona_lnp
 Neoplasms_lnp
 Cardiovasc_lnp
 Chronic_re_lnp
 Digestive_lnp
 Neurologic_lnp
 Mental_dis_lnp
 Substance_lnp
 Diabetes_a_lnp
 Skin_lnp
 Musculoske_lnp
 Other_nonc_lnp
 Transport_lnp
 Unintentio_lnp
 Selfharm_lnp
   /METHOD=ENTER year.
EXECUTE.

** Supplementary table S10.
compute yeargroup=0.
recode yeargroup (0=sysmis).
EXECUTE.
if (year>=1990 and year<=1999) yeargroup=1.
if (year>=2000 and year<=2009) yeargroup=2.
if (year>=2010 and year<=2019) yeargroup=3.
VALUE LABELS yeargroup
1 '1990-1999'
2 '2000-2009'
3 '2010-2019'.
EXECUTE.

USE ALL. 
COMPUTE filter_$=(yeargroup = 1). 
VARIABLE LABELS filter_$ 'yeargroup = 1 (FILTER)'. 
VALUE LABELS filter_$ 0 'Not Selected' 1 'Selected'. 
FORMATS filter_$ (f1.0). 
FILTER BY filter_$. 
EXECUTE.

**supplementary table S11.
*Univaribale model.
* Generalized Estimating Equations.
GENLIN allcausemortality BY HRHgroup (ORDER=ASCENDING) WITH year popul_density urban_percentage 
    schooling gdp SDI HDI
  /MODEL HRHgroup year INTERCEPT=YES
 DISTRIBUTION=GAMMA LINK=LOG
  /CRITERIA METHOD=FISHER(1) SCALE=MLE MAXITERATIONS=100 MAXSTEPHALVING=5 
    PCONVERGE=1E-006(ABSOLUTE) SINGULAR=1E-012 ANALYSISTYPE=3(WALD) CILEVEL=95 LIKELIHOOD=FULL
  /REPEATED SUBJECT=location_id_n WITHINSUBJECT=year SORT=YES CORRTYPE=INDEPENDENT ADJUSTCORR=YES 
    COVB=ROBUST MAXITERATIONS=100 PCONVERGE=1e-006(ABSOLUTE) UPDATECORR=1
  /MISSING CLASSMISSING=EXCLUDE
  /PRINT CPS DESCRIPTIVES MODELINFO FIT SUMMARY SOLUTION (EXPONENTIATED).
EXECUTE.

* Generalized Estimating Equations.
GENLIN allcausemortality BY HRHgroup (ORDER=ASCENDING) WITH year popul_density urban_percentage 
    schooling gdp SDI HDI
  /MODEL year INTERCEPT=YES
 DISTRIBUTION=GAMMA LINK=LOG
  /CRITERIA METHOD=FISHER(1) SCALE=MLE MAXITERATIONS=100 MAXSTEPHALVING=5 
    PCONVERGE=1E-006(ABSOLUTE) SINGULAR=1E-012 ANALYSISTYPE=3(WALD) CILEVEL=95 LIKELIHOOD=FULL
  /REPEATED SUBJECT=location_id_n WITHINSUBJECT=year SORT=YES CORRTYPE=INDEPENDENT ADJUSTCORR=YES 
    COVB=ROBUST MAXITERATIONS=100 PCONVERGE=1e-006(ABSOLUTE) UPDATECORR=1
  /MISSING CLASSMISSING=EXCLUDE
  /PRINT CPS DESCRIPTIVES MODELINFO FIT SUMMARY SOLUTION (EXPONENTIATED).
EXECUTE.

* Generalized Estimating Equations.
GENLIN allcausemortality BY HRHgroup (ORDER=ASCENDING) WITH year popul_density urban_percentage 
    schooling gdp SDI HDI
  /MODEL popul_density year INTERCEPT=YES
 DISTRIBUTION=GAMMA LINK=LOG
  /CRITERIA METHOD=FISHER(1) SCALE=MLE MAXITERATIONS=100 MAXSTEPHALVING=5 
    PCONVERGE=1E-006(ABSOLUTE) SINGULAR=1E-012 ANALYSISTYPE=3(WALD) CILEVEL=95 LIKELIHOOD=FULL
  /REPEATED SUBJECT=location_id_n WITHINSUBJECT=year SORT=YES CORRTYPE=INDEPENDENT ADJUSTCORR=YES 
    COVB=ROBUST MAXITERATIONS=100 PCONVERGE=1e-006(ABSOLUTE) UPDATECORR=1
  /MISSING CLASSMISSING=EXCLUDE

FILTER BY filter_$.

compute Dental_Ass_lnp=LN(Dental_Ass).
compute Dentistry__lnp=LN(Dentistry_).
compute Dentists_lnp=LN(Dentists).
compute Dieticians_lnp=LN(Dieticians).
compute Environmen_lnp=LN(Environmen).
compute Medical_As_lnp=LN(Medical_As).
compute Medical_La_lnp=LN(Medical_La).
compute Nursing___lnp=LN(Nursing__).
compute Nursing_an_lnp=LN(Nursing_an).
compute Optometris_lnp=LN(Optometris).
compute Personal_C_lnp=LN(Personal_C).
compute Pharmaceut_lnp=LN(Pharmaceut).
compute Pharmacist_lnp=LN(Pharmacist).
compute Physical_T_lnp=LN(Physical_T).
compute physicians__mean_lnp=LN(physicians__mean).
compute Physicians_lnp=LN(Physicians).
compute Psychologi_lnp=LN(Psychologi).
compute Radiograph_lnp=LN(Radiograph).
compute Traditiona_lnp=LN(Traditiona).
EXECUTE.

  /MODEL Physical_T_g year popul_density urban_percentage 
    schooling gdp HDI INTERCEPT=YES
 DISTRIBUTION=GAMMA LINK=LOG
  /CRITERIA METHOD=FISHER(1) SCALE=MLE MAXITERATIONS=100 MAXSTEPHALVING=5 
    PCONVERGE=1E-006(ABSOLUTE) SINGULAR=1E-012 ANALYSISTYPE=3(WALD) CILEVEL=95 LIKELIHOOD=FULL
  /REPEATED SUBJECT=location_id_n WITHINSUBJECT=year SORT=YES CORRTYPE=INDEPENDENT ADJUSTCORR=YES 
    COVB=ROBUST MAXITERATIONS=100 PCONVERGE=1e-006(ABSOLUTE) UPDATECORR=1
  /MISSING CLASSMISSING=EXCLUDE
  /PRINT CPS DESCRIPTIVES MODELINFO FIT SUMMARY SOLUTION (EXPONENTIATED).
EXECUTE.

* Custom Tables.
CTABLES
  /VLABELS VARIABLES=HRHgroup Aides__Em_g Audiologis_g Dental_Ass_g Dentistry__g Dentists_g 
    Dieticians_g Environmen_g Medical_As_g Medical_La_g Nursing___g Nursing_an_g Optometris_g 
    Personal_C_g Pharmaceut_g Pharmacist_g Physical_T_g physicians__mean_g Physicians_g Psychologi_g 
    Radiograph_g Traditiona_g allcausemortality 
    DISPLAY=LABEL
  /TABLE HRHgroup + Aides__Em_g + Audiologis_g + Dental_Ass_g + Dentistry__g + Dentists_g + 
    Dieticians_g + Environmen_g + Medical_As_g + Medical_La_g + Nursing___g + Nursing_an_g + 
    Optometris_g + Personal_C_g + Pharmaceut_g + Pharmacist_g + Physical_T_g + physicians__mean_g + 
    Physicians_g + Psychologi_g + Radiograph_g + Traditiona_g BY allcausemortality [S][MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75]
  /CATEGORIES VARIABLES=HRHgroup Aides__Em_g Audiologis_g Dental_Ass_g Dentistry__g Dentists_g 
    Dieticians_g Environmen_g Medical_As_g Medical_La_g Nursing___g Nursing_an_g Optometris_g 
    Personal_C_g Pharmaceut_g Pharmacist_g Physical_T_g physicians__mean_g Physicians_g Psychologi_g 
    Radiograph_g Traditiona_g ORDER=A KEY=VALUE EMPTY=INCLUDE
  /CRITERIA CILEVEL=95.
EXECUTE.

    Nutritiona Neoplasms Cardiovasc Chronic_re Digestive_ Neurologic Mental_dis Substance_ Diabetes_a 
    Skin_and_s Musculoske Other_nonc Transport_ Unintentio Selfharm_a 
    DISPLAY=LABEL

    PTILE 75] + Enteric_in [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neglected_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Other_infe [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Maternal_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Nutritiona 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neoplasms [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Cardiovasc [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Chronic_re [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Digestive_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Neurologic [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Mental_dis [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Substance_ 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Diabetes_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Skin_and_s [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Musculoske [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Other_nonc [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Transport_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Unintentio [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Selfharm_a 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75]
  /CATEGORIES VARIABLES=HRHgroup ORDER=A KEY=VALUE EMPTY=INCLUDE
  /CRITERIA CILEVEL=95.

**supplementary table S6 and supplementary fig S2.
*EAPC for Aides__Em by country.
*1990.
USE ALL. 
COMPUTE filter_$=(year = 1990). 
VARIABLE LABELS filter_$ 'year = 1990 (FILTER)'. 
VALUE LABELS filter_$ 0 'Not Selected' 1 'Selected'. 
FORMATS filter_$ (f1.0). 
FILTER BY filter_$. 
EXECUTE.
* Custom Tables.
CTABLES
  /VLABELS VARIABLES=location_id_n Aides__Em DISPLAY=LABEL
  /TABLE location_id_n [C] BY Aides__Em [MEDIAN]
  /CATEGORIES VARIABLES=location_id_n ORDER=A KEY=VALUE EMPTY=EXCLUDE
  /CRITERIA CILEVEL=95.
EXECUTE.
USE ALL. 
EXECUTE.
*2019.
COMPUTE filter_$=(year = 2019). 
VARIABLE LABELS filter_$ 'year = 2019 (FILTER)'. 
VALUE LABELS filter_$ 0 'Not Selected' 1 'Selected'. 
FORMATS filter_$ (f1.0). 
FILTER BY filter_$. 
EXECUTE.
* Custom Tables.
CTABLES
  /VLABELS VARIABLES=location_id_n Aides__Em DISPLAY=LABEL
  /TABLE location_id_n [C] BY Aides__Em [MEDIAN]
  /CATEGORIES VARIABLES=location_id_n ORDER=A KEY=VALUE EMPTY=EXCLUDE
  /CRITERIA CILEVEL=95.
EXECUTE.
USE ALL. 
EXECUTE.
*EAPC.
SORT CASES  BY location_id_n.
SPLIT FILE LAYERED BY location_id_n.
EXECUTE.
REGRESSION
  /MISSING LISTWISE
  /STATISTICS COEFF OUTS CI(95) R ANOVA
  /CRITERIA=PIN(.05) POUT(.10)
  /NOORIGIN 
  /DEPENDENT 
Aides__Em_lnp
   /METHOD=ENTER year.
EXECUTE.
SPLIT FILE OFF.
EXECUTE.
*EAPC for Audiologis by country.
*1990.
USE ALL. 
COMPUTE filter_$=(year = 1990).

*supplementary table S12.
*Univaribale model.
* Generalized Estimating Equations.
GENLIN allcausemortality BY Aides__Em_g (ORDER=ASCENDING) WITH year popul_density urban_percentage 
    schooling gdp SDI HDI
  /MODEL Aides__Em_g year INTERCEPT=YES
 DISTRIBUTION=GAMMA LINK=LOG
  /CRITERIA METHOD=FISHER(1) SCALE=MLE MAXITERATIONS=100 MAXSTEPHALVING=5 
    PCONVERGE=1E-006(ABSOLUTE) SINGULAR=1E-012 ANALYSISTYPE=3(WALD) CILEVEL=95 LIKELIHOOD=FULL
  /REPEATED SUBJECT=location_id_n WITHINSUBJECT=year SORT=YES CORRTYPE=INDEPENDENT ADJUSTCORR=YES 
    COVB=ROBUST MAXITERATIONS=100 PCONVERGE=1e-006(ABSOLUTE) UPDATECORR=1
  /MISSING CLASSMISSING=EXCLUDE
  /PRINT CPS DESCRIPTIVES MODELINFO FIT SUMMARY SOLUTION (EXPONENTIATED).
EXECUTE.

    Nutritiona Neoplasms Cardiovasc Chronic_re Digestive_ Neurologic Mental_dis Substance_ Diabetes_a 
    Skin_and_s Musculoske Other_nonc Transport_ Unintentio Selfharm_a

  /TABLE Dentistry__g [C] BY HIV_AIDS_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Respirator [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, 
    PTILE 75] + Enteric_in [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neglected_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Other_infe [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Maternal_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Nutritiona 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neoplasms [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Cardiovasc [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Chronic_re [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Digestive_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Neurologic [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Mental_dis [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Substance_ 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Diabetes_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Skin_and_s [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Musculoske [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Other_nonc [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Transport_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Unintentio [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Selfharm_a 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75]

  /CRITERIA CILEVEL=95.

* Custom Tables.
CTABLES
  /VLABELS VARIABLES=Pharmaceut_g HIV_AIDS_a Respirator Enteric_in Neglected_ Other_infe Maternal_a 
    Nutritiona Neoplasms Cardiovasc Chronic_re Digestive_ Neurologic Mental_dis Substance_ Diabetes_a 
    Skin_and_s Musculoske Other_nonc Transport_ Unintentio Selfharm_a 
    DISPLAY=LABEL
  /TABLE Pharmaceut_g [C] BY HIV_AIDS_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Respirator [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, 
    PTILE 75] + Enteric_in [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neglected_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Other_infe [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Maternal_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Nutritiona 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neoplasms [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Cardiovasc [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Chronic_re [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Digestive_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Neurologic [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Mental_dis [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Substance_ 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Diabetes_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Skin_and_s [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Musculoske [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Other_nonc [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Transport_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Unintentio [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Selfharm_a 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75]
  /CATEGORIES VARIABLES=Pharmaceut_g ORDER=A KEY=VALUE EMPTY=INCLUDE
  /CRITERIA CILEVEL=95.
EXECUTE.

**supplementary fig S7.
* Custom Tables.
CTABLES
  /VLABELS VARIABLES=Medical_As_g HIV_AIDS_a Respirator Enteric_in Neglected_ Other_infe Maternal_a 
    Nutritiona Neoplasms Cardiovasc Chronic_re Digestive_ Neurologic Mental_dis Substance_ Diabetes_a 
    Skin_and_s Musculoske Other_nonc Transport_ Unintentio Selfharm_a 
    DISPLAY=LABEL
  /TABLE Medical_As_g [C] BY HIV_AIDS_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Respirator [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, 
    PTILE 75] + Enteric_in [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neglected_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Other_infe [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Maternal_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Nutritiona 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neoplasms [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Cardiovasc [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Chronic_re [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Digestive_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Neurologic [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Mental_dis [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Substance_ 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Diabetes_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Skin_and_s [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Musculoske [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Other_nonc [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Transport_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Unintentio [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Selfharm_a 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75]
  /CATEGORIES VARIABLES=Medical_As_g ORDER=A KEY=VALUE EMPTY=INCLUDE
  /CRITERIA CILEVEL=95.
EXECUTE.

* Custom Tables.
CTABLES
  /VLABELS VARIABLES=Aides__Em_g HIV_AIDS_a Respirator Enteric_in Neglected_ Other_infe Maternal_a 
    Nutritiona Neoplasms Cardiovasc Chronic_re Digestive_ Neurologic Mental_dis Substance_ Diabetes_a 
    Skin_and_s Musculoske Other_nonc Transport_ Unintentio Selfharm_a 
    DISPLAY=LABEL
  /TABLE Aides__Em_g [C] BY HIV_AIDS_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Respirator [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, 
    PTILE 75] + Enteric_in [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neglected_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Other_infe [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Maternal_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Nutritiona 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neoplasms [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Cardiovasc [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Chronic_re [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Digestive_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Neurologic [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Mental_dis [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Substance_ 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Diabetes_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Skin_and_s [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Musculoske [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Other_nonc [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Transport_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Unintentio [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Selfharm_a 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75]
  /CATEGORIES VARIABLES=Aides__Em_g ORDER=A KEY=VALUE EMPTY=INCLUDE
  /CRITERIA CILEVEL=95.
EXECUTE.

* Custom Tables.
CTABLES
  /VLABELS VARIABLES=Medical_La_g HIV_AIDS_a Respirator Enteric_in Neglected_ Other_infe Maternal_a 
    Nutritiona Neoplasms Cardiovasc Chronic_re Digestive_ Neurologic Mental_dis Substance_ Diabetes_a 
    Skin_and_s Musculoske Other_nonc Transport_ Unintentio Selfharm_a 
    DISPLAY=LABEL
  /TABLE Medical_La_g [C] BY HIV_AIDS_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Respirator [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, 
    PTILE 75] + Enteric_in [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neglected_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Other_infe [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Maternal_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Nutritiona 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neoplasms [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Cardiovasc [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Chronic_re [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Digestive_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Neurologic [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Mental_dis [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Substance_ 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Diabetes_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Skin_and_s [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Musculoske [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Other_nonc [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Transport_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Unintentio [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Selfharm_a 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75]
  /CATEGORIES VARIABLES=Medical_La_g ORDER=A KEY=VALUE EMPTY=INCLUDE
  /CRITERIA CILEVEL=95.
EXECUTE.

* Generalized Estimating Equations.

    schooling gdp SDI HDI
  /MODEL Medical_La_g year popul_density urban_percentage 
    schooling gdp HDI INTERCEPT=YES
 DISTRIBUTION=GAMMA LINK=LOG

    COVB=ROBUST MAXITERATIONS=100 PCONVERGE=1e-006(ABSOLUTE) UPDATECORR=1

  /PRINT CPS DESCRIPTIVES MODELINFO FIT SUMMARY SOLUTION (EXPONENTIATED).

    COVB=ROBUST MAXITERATIONS=100 PCONVERGE=1e-006(ABSOLUTE) UPDATECORR=1
  /MISSING CLASSMISSING=EXCLUDE
  /PRINT CPS DESCRIPTIVES MODELINFO FIT SUMMARY SOLUTION (EXPONENTIATED).

**supplementary fig S12.
* Custom Tables.
CTABLES
  /VLABELS VARIABLES=Audiologis_g HIV_AIDS_a Respirator Enteric_in Neglected_ Other_infe Maternal_a 
    Nutritiona Neoplasms Cardiovasc Chronic_re Digestive_ Neurologic Mental_dis Substance_ Diabetes_a 
    Skin_and_s Musculoske Other_nonc Transport_ Unintentio Selfharm_a 
    DISPLAY=LABEL
  /TABLE Audiologis_g [C] BY HIV_AIDS_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Respirator [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, 
    PTILE 75] + Enteric_in [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neglected_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Other_infe [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Maternal_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Nutritiona 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neoplasms [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Cardiovasc [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Chronic_re [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Digestive_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Neurologic [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Mental_dis [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Substance_ 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Diabetes_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Skin_and_s [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Musculoske [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Other_nonc [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Transport_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Unintentio [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Selfharm_a 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75]
  /CATEGORIES VARIABLES=Audiologis_g ORDER=A KEY=VALUE EMPTY=INCLUDE
  /CRITERIA CILEVEL=95.
EXECUTE.

* Custom Tables.
CTABLES
  /VLABELS VARIABLES=Psychologi_g HIV_AIDS_a Respirator Enteric_in Neglected_ Other_infe Maternal_a 
    Nutritiona Neoplasms Cardiovasc Chronic_re Digestive_ Neurologic Mental_dis Substance_ Diabetes_a 
    Skin_and_s Musculoske Other_nonc Transport_ Unintentio Selfharm_a 
    DISPLAY=LABEL
  /TABLE Psychologi_g [C] BY HIV_AIDS_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Respirator [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, 
    PTILE 75] + Enteric_in [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neglected_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Other_infe [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Maternal_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Nutritiona 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neoplasms [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Cardiovasc [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Chronic_re [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Digestive_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Neurologic [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Mental_dis [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Substance_ 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Diabetes_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Skin_and_s [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Musculoske [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Other_nonc [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Transport_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Unintentio [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Selfharm_a 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75]
  /CATEGORIES VARIABLES=Psychologi_g ORDER=A KEY=VALUE EMPTY=INCLUDE
  /CRITERIA CILEVEL=95.
EXECUTE.

* Custom Tables.
CTABLES
  /VLABELS VARIABLES=Environmen_g HIV_AIDS_a Respirator Enteric_in Neglected_ Other_infe Maternal_a 
    Nutritiona Neoplasms Cardiovasc Chronic_re Digestive_ Neurologic Mental_dis Substance_ Diabetes_a 
    Skin_and_s Musculoske Other_nonc Transport_ Unintentio Selfharm_a 
    DISPLAY=LABEL
  /TABLE Environmen_g [C] BY HIV_AIDS_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Respirator [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, 
    PTILE 75] + Enteric_in [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neglected_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Other_infe [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Maternal_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Nutritiona 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neoplasms [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Cardiovasc [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Chronic_re [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Digestive_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Neurologic [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Mental_dis [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Substance_ 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Diabetes_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Skin_and_s [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Musculoske [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Other_nonc [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Transport_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Unintentio [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Selfharm_a 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75]
  /CATEGORIES VARIABLES=Environmen_g ORDER=A KEY=VALUE EMPTY=INCLUDE
  /CRITERIA CILEVEL=95.
EXECUTE.

* Custom Tables.
CTABLES
  /VLABELS VARIABLES=Personal_C_g HIV_AIDS_a Respirator Enteric_in Neglected_ Other_infe Maternal_a 
    Nutritiona Neoplasms Cardiovasc Chronic_re Digestive_ Neurologic Mental_dis Substance_ Diabetes_a 
    Skin_and_s Musculoske Other_nonc Transport_ Unintentio Selfharm_a 
    DISPLAY=LABEL
  /TABLE Personal_C_g [C] BY HIV_AIDS_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Respirator [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, 
    PTILE 75] + Enteric_in [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neglected_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Other_infe [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Maternal_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Nutritiona 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neoplasms [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Cardiovasc [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Chronic_re [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Digestive_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Neurologic [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Mental_dis [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Substance_ 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Diabetes_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Skin_and_s [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Musculoske [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Other_nonc [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Transport_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Unintentio [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Selfharm_a 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75]
  /CATEGORIES VARIABLES=Personal_C_g ORDER=A KEY=VALUE EMPTY=INCLUDE
  /CRITERIA CILEVEL=95.
EXECUTE.

GENLIN HIV_AIDS_a BY Physical_T_g (ORDER=ASCENDING) WITH year popul_density urban_percentage 
    schooling gdp SDI HDI
  /MODEL Physical_T_g year popul_density urban_percentage 
    schooling gdp HDI INTERCEPT=YES
 DISTRIBUTION=GAMMA LINK=LOG
  /CRITERIA METHOD=FISHER(1) SCALE=MLE MAXITERATIONS=100 MAXSTEPHALVING=5 
    PCONVERGE=1E-006(ABSOLUTE) SINGULAR=1E-012 ANALYSISTYPE=3(WALD) CILEVEL=95 LIKELIHOOD=FULL
  /REPEATED SUBJECT=location_id_n WITHINSUBJECT=year SORT=YES CORRTYPE=INDEPENDENT ADJUSTCORR=YES 
    COVB=ROBUST MAXITERATIONS=100 PCONVERGE=1e-006(ABSOLUTE) UPDATECORR=1
  /MISSING CLASSMISSING=EXCLUDE
  /PRINT CPS DESCRIPTIVES MODELINFO FIT SUMMARY SOLUTION (EXPONENTIATED).
EXECUTE.

**supplementary fig S18.
* Custom Tables.
CTABLES
  /VLABELS VARIABLES=Radiograph_g HIV_AIDS_a Respirator Enteric_in Neglected_ Other_infe Maternal_a 
    Nutritiona Neoplasms Cardiovasc Chronic_re Digestive_ Neurologic Mental_dis Substance_ Diabetes_a 
    Skin_and_s Musculoske Other_nonc Transport_ Unintentio Selfharm_a 
    DISPLAY=LABEL
  /TABLE Radiograph_g [C] BY HIV_AIDS_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Respirator [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, 
    PTILE 75] + Enteric_in [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neglected_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Other_infe [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Maternal_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Nutritiona 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Neoplasms [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Cardiovasc [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Chronic_re [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Digestive_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Neurologic [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Mental_dis [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Substance_ 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Diabetes_a [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Skin_and_s [MEDIAN, PTILE 
    25, PTILE 75] + Musculoske [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Other_nonc [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + 
    Transport_ [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Unintentio [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75] + Selfharm_a 
    [MEDIAN, PTILE 25, PTILE 75]
  /CATEGORIES VARIABLES=Radiograph_g ORDER=A KEY=VALUE EMPTY=INCLUDE
  /CRITERIA CILEVEL=95.
EXECUTE.

* Generalized Estimating Equations.
GENLIN HIV_AIDS_a BY Radiograph_g (ORDER=ASCENDING) WITH year popul_density urban_percentage 
    schooling gdp SDI HDI
  /MODEL Radiograph_g year popul_density urban_percentage 
    schooling gdp HDI INTERCEPT=YES
 DISTRIBUTION=GAMMA LINK=LOG
  /CRITERIA METHOD=FISHER(1) SCALE=MLE MAXITERATIONS=100 MAXSTEPHALVING=5 
    PCONVERGE=1E-006(ABSOLUTE) SINGULAR=1E-012 ANALYSISTYPE=3(WALD) CILEVEL=95 LIKELIHOOD=FULL
  /REPEATED SUBJECT=location_id_n WITHINSUBJECT=year SORT=YES CORRTYPE=INDEPENDENT ADJUSTCORR=YES 
    COVB=ROBUST MAXITERATIONS=100 PCONVERGE=1e-006(ABSOLUTE) UPDATECORR=1
  /MISSING CLASSMISSING=EXCLUDE
  /PRINT CPS DESCRIPTIVES MODELINFO FIT SUMMARY SOLUTION (EXPONENTIATED).
